<rating>2</rating>< review>
I went to Dr. Lee because I had a "TMJ Disorder" and his website said he did a fellowship focusing on TMJ.  My jaw was locked to the point that I could only open it two finger widths. Dr. Lee did all that he could to treat it without surgery, which I liked.  He gave me a splint that I wore 24/7 for about 6 months and then just at night as the pain went away.  Every visit I had, Dr. Lee asked me how the pain was.  It was getting better every time.  Now there is no pain and I still wear the splint at night but my bite is very off.  None of my right teeth touch.  I can't rip or tear with my teeth.  My jaw still locks but it unlocks.  My new dentist suggested that I get braces now to realign my bite and hopefully relieve my jaw. I cannot speak on any other procedure that Dr. Lee performs but for problems with TMJ, go somewhere else.  The pain was treated but the problem persisted and led to other problems.< /review>

< review>
Update 12/2/2020. The hospital responded to my email and is working on my concerns. Placentia-Linda has exceptional doctors and nursing staff. My one star rating is for the administrative staff and billing department. For 25 years my family has utilized the services of this hospital from the birth of our children, to orthopedic procedures, and other medical needs, both minor and major.  In all cases we were very happy. The most recent visit occurred in May 2019 for a CT scan.  The hospital billed both my primary and secondary insurance, both of whom paid. When it was my turn to pay my portion, an error in the billing to the insurance was discovered.  The hospital and Anthem went back and forth for over a year. I got involved and during a three way call Placentia Linda admitted the billing error, made the correction, and confirmed a zero balance.  I was informed I would be getting a statement confirming the payment.  Two weeks later the statement arrived with an even larger balance. I attempted to reach out to the billing manager (no response) and the hospital administrators office (they responded but never followed up).  Again the doctors and nursing staff are the best; however, the administrators and lack of communication by them and the billing department will cause me hesitation in considering a visit to this hospital in the future.< /review>

They said they couldn't that Dr. Cole was the one on call. I was given more and more drugs to sedate the pain and the clock was just going by. 4am, 5am still nothing I felt as if I was being stabbed on a constant. Still nothing 7am begging the hospital to help me and to call somebody else a nurse in the hospital explained to me that Dr. Cole likes his sleep. I had a fever and by the 5th day got Dr. Cole to agree to see me. I waited another two days for my appointment. <user_name>Tod Imperato</user_name><Rating>5<//Rating>< text>
My discovery of this gem was a happy accident. I got stopped by traffic turning into the In-N-Out and my wife spied Vinoma tucked in next to it. I stopped by and the chef met me at the door (no dine-in at this time due to pandemic) and told me all about the menu. It includes traditional closed empanadas and open-faced versions with a variety of toppings and flavors. There are also breakfast and dessert items. I tried some of almost everything (there is a lower unit price for a dozen+) and all of them were delicious. The plum & bacon was wonderful, ditto the al pastor. Meatless Caprese, creamy corn, and spinach artichoke varieties were also highly yummy. I've spent a good deal of time in Argentina and these are authentic. The natural sodas are tasty too. The chef was friendly and helpful and I will definitely be back.</text>

<Rate>5</Rate>< Review>
In my dozen plus dining experiences at the Parkfield Cafe they were extraordinary. No matter the choices from the menu, each and every item from a simple hamburger, divine salads, a steak to die for or ribs beyond compare makes the going well worth it.

Though as to service, it too is beyond compare.  The staff are locals, very friendly, helpful and see to every last detail to make every customer feel welcome and well cared for.

So forget those high prized jazzy places because Parkfield has it all and if you're lucky, you'll get a shake with your meal too!< /Review>

< text>
Their all-you-can-eat buffet is great! They have alot of different pizzas, fried & roasted chicken, both are great! Plus other entrees and sides and a nice salad bar. This is not a high end buffet but I like it. Their people are friendly and eager to help. They have 4 or 5 large tv's in the main dining area (if there is an event you want to see, all you have to do is ask...they have the Dodger channel), an area for reserved parties and a game room that the kids seem to love. All-in-all it's a great place to have a meal and take the load off, enjoy some good food and watch a game.<//text>
